Hello, List!
Here are the listings as of May 28, 2014.


Listings Project Story of the Week:
Just wanted to drop you a quick line and say thanks for doing all that you do with the Listings Project and for all the many wonderful ways it has helped connect people! Within a week of posting our space, we found the perfect tenants for our space, which allowed us to make the big move from Bushwick to the East Village. Our tenants are happy, and so are we. The move has been life changing and has really made our experience in NYC so much more enjoyable! Keep up the good work, and while I'm not looking forward to our next move (some years down the road hopefully), I will for sure explore LP for options! -Heidi


Best,
Stephanie
